## ğŸš¨ OTOMATÄ°K RED DURUMLARI ve SONUÃ‡LARI

### Seviye 2: BLOKE (Blocked)

## ğŸ”Œ API KONTRATI

## ğŸ”’ GÃœVENLÄ°K GEREKSÄ°NÄ°MLERÄ°

### 1. Ä°letiÅŸim GÃ¼venliÄŸi
- **Protokol:** HTTPS (TLS 1.3)
- **Certificate Pinning:** Zorunlu (production'da)
- **Request Signing:** HMAC-SHA256 ile imzalama

### 2. Kimlik DoÄŸrulama
- **Primary:** OAuth 2.0 Bearer Token
- **Fallback:** API Key (sadece development)
- **Token Rotation:** Her 1 saatte bir yenilenmelidir

### 3. Veri Åifreleme
- **Transit:** TLS 1.3
- **Rest:** AES-256-GCM (hassas veriler iÃ§in)
- **Key Management:** Android Keystore kullanÄ±lmalÄ±dÄ±r

### 4. Rate Limiting
- **Maksimum:** 100 request/dakika
- **Burst:** 20 request/saniye
- **Retry Policy:** Exponential backoff (1s, 2s, 4s, 8s)

---

## ğŸ’¾ CACHE STRATEJÄ°SÄ°

### Cache KatmanlarÄ±

1. **Memory Cache (L1):** SÄ±k eriÅŸilen veriler (TTL: 5 dakika)
2. **Disk Cache (L2):** Orta sÄ±klÄ±kta eriÅŸilen veriler (TTL: 1 saat)
3. **Database Cache (L3):** Nadiren deÄŸiÅŸen veriler (TTL: 24 saat)

### Cache Invalidation
```kotlin
// Otomatik invalidation
- Yeni veri geldiÄŸinde
- TTL dolduÄŸunda
- KullanÄ±cÄ± logout olduÄŸunda

// Manuel invalidation
fun clearKorlukGlobalCache() {
    memoryCache.clear()
    diskCache.clear()
    databaseCache.clear()
}
```

## âš ï¸ HATA YÃ–NETÄ°MÄ°

### Hata SenaryolarÄ± ve Ã‡Ã¶zÃ¼mler

#### Senaryo 1: KÃ–RLÃœKGLOBAL EriÅŸilemez
```kotlin
try {
    val response = korlukGlobalApi.fetchData()
    // BaÅŸarÄ±lÄ±
} catch (e: IOException) {
    // Network hatasÄ± - cache'ten veri sun
    return cacheManager.getLastKnownData() ?: emptyData()
}
```

#### Senaryo 2: Kimlik DoÄŸrulama HatasÄ±
```kotlin
if (response.code == 401) {
    // Token geÃ§ersiz, yenile
    tokenManager.refreshToken()
    // Retry
    return korlukGlobalApi.fetchData()
}
```

#### Senaryo 3: Rate Limit AÅŸÄ±mÄ±
```kotlin
if (response.code == 429) {
    // Retry-After header'Ä± kontrol et
    val retryAfter = response.headers["Retry-After"]?.toInt() ?: 60
    delay(retryAfter * 1000L)
    // Retry
}
```

#### Senaryo 4: Sunucu HatasÄ± (5xx)
```kotlin
if (response.code in 500..599) {
    // Exponential backoff
    repeat(3) { attempt ->
        delay(2.0.pow(attempt).toLong() * 1000)
        val retry = korlukGlobalApi.fetchData()
        if (retry.isSuccessful) return retry
    }
    // Son Ã§are: cache'ten sun
    return cacheManager.getLastKnownData()
}
```

```bash
# Versiyon: 1.0

echo "ğŸ›ï¸ Anayasa Uygunluk KontrolÃ¼ BaÅŸlÄ±yor..."

VIOLATIONS=0

    echo "âŒ HATA: Anayasa dosyasÄ± bulunamadÄ±!"
    exit 1

    -exec grep -L "Sorumlu:" {} \;)

    echo "   âŒ Sorumlu belirtilmemiÅŸ belgeler:"
    echo "$FILES_WITHOUT_OWNER" | while read file; do
        echo "      - $file"
        ((VIOLATIONS++))
    done

    echo "   âŒ HATA: evidence/ klasÃ¶rÃ¼ bulunamadÄ±!"
    ((VIOLATIONS++))

    if [ $EVIDENCE_COUNT -eq 0 ]; then
        echo "   âš ï¸  UYARI: evidence/ klasÃ¶rÃ¼ boÅŸ!"
        ((VIOLATIONS++))
    else
        echo "   âœ… $EVIDENCE_COUNT adet kanÄ±t dosyasÄ± mevcut"
    fi

# DenetÃ§i yorumlarÄ± var mÄ±?

    -exec grep -l "DenetÃ§i.*:" {} \; | wc -l)

if [ $DENETCI_COMMENTS -gt 0 ]; then
    echo "   âœ… $DENETCI_COMMENTS belgede denetÃ§i yorumu bulundu"
else
    echo "   âš ï¸  UYARI: HiÃ§bir belgede denetÃ§i yorumu yok"

# Madde 4: Belge HiyerarÅŸisi KutsaldÄ±r - KontrolÃ¼
echo ""

echo "   HiyerarÅŸi belgesi kontrol ediliyor..."

    echo "   âŒ HATA: HiyerarÅŸi belgesi bulunamadÄ±!"
    ((VIOLATIONS++))

    echo "âœ… BAÅARILI: Anayasa uygunluk kontrolÃ¼ geÃ§ildi"
    echo "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•"
```

### Script: `validate_document_hierarchy.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# PATIDOST Belge HiyerarÅŸisi KontrolÃ¼
# Versiyon: 1.0

echo "ğŸ“š Belge HiyerarÅŸisi KontrolÃ¼ BaÅŸlÄ±yor..."

VIOLATIONS=0

# Merkezi kayÄ±t deposunu kontrol et
REGISTRY_FILE="contracts/CENTRAL_REGISTRY_INDEX.md"

if [ ! -f "$REGISTRY_FILE" ]; then
    echo "âŒ HATA: Merkezi kayÄ±t deposu bulunamadÄ±!"
    exit 1
fi

echo "âœ… Merkezi kayÄ±t deposu bulundu"

# TÃ¼m MD dosyalarÄ±nÄ± bul
ALL_DOCS=$(find docs contracts -name "*.md" -type f ! -name "*_DRAFT*")

# Her belgenin kayÄ±t deposunda olup olmadÄ±ÄŸÄ±nÄ± kontrol et
echo ""
echo "ğŸ“‹ KayÄ±t deposu kontrolÃ¼..."
UNREGISTERED=0

for doc in $ALL_DOCS; do
    DOC_NAME=$(basename "$doc")
    if ! grep -q "$DOC_NAME" "$REGISTRY_FILE"; then
        echo "   âš ï¸  KayÄ±t dÄ±ÅŸÄ± belge: $doc"
        ((UNREGISTERED++))
        ((VIOLATIONS++))
    fi
done

if [ $UNREGISTERED -eq 0 ]; then
    echo "   âœ… TÃ¼m belgeler kayÄ±t deposunda mevcut"
else
    echo "   âŒ $UNREGISTERED belge kayÄ±t dÄ±ÅŸÄ±"

# Belge sÄ±nÄ±flandÄ±rmasÄ± kontrolÃ¼
echo ""
echo "ğŸ“Š Belge sÄ±nÄ±flandÄ±rmasÄ± kontrolÃ¼..."
UNCLASSIFIED=0

    # Belge iÃ§inde "Anayasal StatÃ¼" veya "Seviye" etiketi var mÄ±?
    if ! grep -q -E "(Anayasal StatÃ¼:|Seviye:)" "$doc"; then
        echo "   âš ï¸  SÄ±nÄ±flandÄ±rÄ±lmamÄ±ÅŸ belge: $doc"
        ((UNCLASSIFIED++))
        ((VIOLATIONS++))
    fi
done

if [ $UNCLASSIFIED -eq 0 ]; then
    echo "   âœ… TÃ¼m belgeler sÄ±nÄ±flandÄ±rÄ±lmÄ±ÅŸ"
else
    echo "   âŒ $UNCLASSIFIED belge sÄ±nÄ±flandÄ±rÄ±lmamÄ±ÅŸ"
fi

# Ã‡eliÅŸki kontrolÃ¼ (basit versiyon)
echo ""
echo "ğŸ” Ã‡eliÅŸki tespiti..."
# AynÄ± konuda farklÄ± versiyonlar var mÄ±?
DUPLICATES=$(find docs contracts -name "*.md" -type f \
    | sed 's/_v[0-9]\+\.[0-9]\+\.md$//' \
    | sort | uniq -d)

if [ -n "$DUPLICATES" ]; then
    echo "   âš ï¸  Potansiyel Ã§eliÅŸkili belgeler tespit edildi:"
    echo "$DUPLICATES"
    echo "   (Manuel inceleme Ã¶nerilir)"
else
    echo "   âœ… AÃ§Ä±k Ã§eliÅŸki tespit edilmedi"
fi

# SONUÃ‡
echo ""
echo "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•"
if [ $VIOLATIONS -eq 0 ]; then
    echo "âœ… BAÅARILI: Belge hiyerarÅŸisi kontrolÃ¼ geÃ§ildi"
    echo "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•"
    exit 0
```

## ğŸ” KATMAN 3: SÃ–ZLEÅME BÃœTÃœNLÃœÄÃœ KONTROLÃœ

### Script: `validate_contract_integrity.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# PATIDOST SÃ¶zleÅŸme BÃ¼tÃ¼nlÃ¼ÄŸÃ¼ KontrolÃ¼
# Versiyon: 1.0

echo "ğŸ“œ SÃ¶zleÅŸme BÃ¼tÃ¼nlÃ¼ÄŸÃ¼ KontrolÃ¼ BaÅŸlÄ±yor..."

VIOLATIONS=0

# Kritik sÃ¶zleÅŸmelerin varlÄ±ÄŸÄ±nÄ± kontrol et
CRITICAL_CONTRACTS=(
    "contracts/backend/API_CONTRACT_v2.md"
    "contracts/backend/DATABASE_SCHEMA_v2.md"
    "contracts/security/SECURITY_MODEL_v2.md"
    "contracts/ux/UI_UX_CONTRACT.md"
)

echo ""
echo "ğŸ” Kritik sÃ¶zleÅŸmeler kontrolÃ¼..."
for contract in "${CRITICAL_CONTRACTS[@]}"; do
    if [ ! -f "$contract" ]; then
        echo "   âŒ EKSÄ°K: $contract"
        ((VIOLATIONS++))
    else
        echo "   âœ… MEVCUT: $contract"
    fi
done

# ModÃ¼l DNA dosyalarÄ±nÄ± kontrol et
echo ""
echo "ğŸ§¬ ModÃ¼l DNA kontrolÃ¼..."
MODULE_DNA_DIR="contracts/modules"

if [ ! -d "$MODULE_DNA_DIR" ]; then
    echo "   âŒ HATA: ModÃ¼l DNA klasÃ¶rÃ¼ bulunamadÄ±!"
    ((VIOLATIONS++))
else
    MODULE_COUNT=$(find $MODULE_DNA_DIR -name "MODULE_DNA_*.md" | wc -l)
    echo "   ğŸ“Š $MODULE_COUNT modÃ¼l DNA dosyasÄ± bulundu"
    
    # En az 5 modÃ¼l bekleniyor
    if [ $MODULE_COUNT -lt 5 ]; then
        echo "   âš ï¸  UYARI: ModÃ¼l sayÄ±sÄ± beklenenden az (minimum 5)"
        ((VIOLATIONS++))
    fi
fi

# API kontratÄ± ile kod uyumluluÄŸu (basit kontrol)
echo ""
echo "ğŸ”Œ API kontratÄ± uyumluluk kontrolÃ¼..."
API_CONTRACT="contracts/backend/API_CONTRACT_v2.md"

if [ -f "$API_CONTRACT" ]; then
    # API dosyasÄ±nda tanÄ±mlÄ± endpoint'leri bul
    ENDPOINTS=$(grep -oP '(?<=GET |POST |PUT |DELETE |PATCH )/\S+' "$API_CONTRACT" | sort -u)
    
    # ApiService.kt dosyasÄ±nÄ± kontrol et
    API_SERVICE_FILE=$(find . -name "ApiService.kt" -type f)
    
    if [ -n "$API_SERVICE_FILE" ]; then
        echo "   âœ… ApiService.kt bulundu: $API_SERVICE_FILE"
        
        # Her endpoint iÃ§in fonksiyon var mÄ± kontrol et
        MISSING_ENDPOINTS=0
        while IFS= read -r endpoint; do
            # Endpoint'i fonksiyon adÄ±na Ã§evir (basit versiyon)
            FUNCTION_NAME=$(echo "$endpoint" | tr '/' '_' | tr '[:upper:]' '[:lower:]')
            
            if ! grep -q "$FUNCTION_NAME" "$API_SERVICE_FILE"; then
                echo "   âš ï¸  Potansiyel eksik endpoint: $endpoint"
                ((MISSING_ENDPOINTS++))
            fi
        done <<< "$ENDPOINTS"
        
        if [ $MISSING_ENDPOINTS -eq 0 ]; then
            echo "   âœ… TÃ¼m endpoint'ler implement edilmiÅŸ gÃ¶rÃ¼nÃ¼yor"
        else
            echo "   âš ï¸  $MISSING_ENDPOINTS endpoint eksik olabilir (manuel kontrol Ã¶nerilir)"
        fi
    else
        echo "   âš ï¸  UYARI: ApiService.kt bulunamadÄ±"
    fi
fi

# SONUÃ‡
echo ""
echo "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•"
if [ $VIOLATIONS -eq 0 ]; then
    echo "âœ… BAÅARILI: SÃ¶zleÅŸme bÃ¼tÃ¼nlÃ¼ÄŸÃ¼ kontrolÃ¼ geÃ§ildi"
    echo "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•"
    exit 0
else
    echo "âŒ BAÅARISIZ: $VIOLATIONS adet sÃ¶zleÅŸme ihlali tespit edildi"
    echo "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•"
    exit 1
fi
```

## ğŸ” KATMAN 4: MODÃœL TUTARLILIÄI KONTROLÃœ

### Script: `validate_module_consistency.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# PATIDOST ModÃ¼l TutarlÄ±lÄ±ÄŸÄ± KontrolÃ¼
# Versiyon: 1.0

echo "ğŸ§© ModÃ¼l TutarlÄ±lÄ±ÄŸÄ± KontrolÃ¼ BaÅŸlÄ±yor..."

VIOLATIONS=0

# Build.gradle.kts dosyalarÄ±nÄ± bul
BUILD_FILES=$(find . -name "build.gradle.kts" -type f)

echo ""
echo "ğŸ“¦ ModÃ¼l baÄŸÄ±mlÄ±lÄ±klarÄ± kontrolÃ¼..."

# Circular dependency kontrolÃ¼
echo "   ğŸ”„ Circular dependency kontrolÃ¼..."
# (Bu basit bir implementasyon, gerÃ§ek projede daha geliÅŸmiÅŸ bir tool kullanÄ±lmalÄ±)

CIRCULAR_FOUND=0
for build_file in $BUILD_FILES; do
    MODULE_NAME=$(dirname "$build_file" | xargs basename)
    
    # Bu modÃ¼lÃ¼n baÄŸÄ±mlÄ±lÄ±klarÄ±nÄ± bul
    DEPS=$(grep -oP "(?<=implementation\(project\(\")[^\"]+(?=\"\)\))" "$build_file")
    
    # Her baÄŸÄ±mlÄ±lÄ±k iÃ§in geri baÄŸÄ±mlÄ±lÄ±k var mÄ± kontrol et
    for dep in $DEPS; do
        DEP_BUILD_FILE=$(find . -path "*${dep#:}/build.gradle.kts" -type f)
        if [ -f "$DEP_BUILD_FILE" ]; then
            if grep -q "implementation(project(\":$MODULE_NAME\"))" "$DEP_BUILD_FILE"; then
                echo "   âŒ CIRCULAR DEPENDENCY: $MODULE_NAME <-> $dep"
                ((CIRCULAR_FOUND++))
                ((VIOLATIONS++))
            fi
        fi
    done
done

if [ $CIRCULAR_FOUND -eq 0 ]; then
    echo "   âœ… Circular dependency tespit edilmedi"
else
    echo "   âŒ $CIRCULAR_FOUND circular dependency tespit edildi"
fi

# Version katalog tutarlÄ±lÄ±ÄŸÄ±
echo ""
echo "ğŸ“š Version katalog kontrolÃ¼..."
VERSION_CATALOG="gradle/libs.versions.toml"

if [ ! -f "$VERSION_CATALOG" ]; then
    echo "   âŒ HATA: libs.versions.toml bulunamadÄ±!"
    ((VIOLATIONS++))
else
    echo "   âœ… Version katalog bulundu"
    
    # TÃ¼m build dosyalarÄ±nda katalog kullanÄ±lÄ±yor mu?
    for build_file in $BUILD_FILES; do
        # Hardcoded version var mÄ±?
        HARDCODED=$(grep -oP 'implementation\(".*:.*:[0-9]+\.[0-9]+' "$build_file")
        if [ -n "$HARDCODED" ]; then
            echo "   âš ï¸  Hardcoded version tespit edildi: $build_file"
            echo "      $HARDCODED"
        fi
    done
fi

# SONUÃ‡
echo ""
echo "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•"
if [ $VIOLATIONS -eq 0 ]; then
    echo "âœ… BAÅARILI: ModÃ¼l tutarlÄ±lÄ±ÄŸÄ± kontrolÃ¼ geÃ§ildi"
    echo "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•"
    exit 0
else
    echo "âŒ BAÅARISIZ: $VIOLATIONS adet modÃ¼l ihlali tespit edildi"
    echo "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•"
    exit 1
fi
```

## ğŸ” KATMAN 5: KOD KALÄ°TESÄ° VE GÃœVENLÄ°K KONTROLÃœ

### Script: `validate_code_quality_security.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# PATIDOST Kod Kalitesi ve GÃ¼venlik KontrolÃ¼
# Versiyon: 1.0

echo "ğŸ”’ Kod Kalitesi ve GÃ¼venlik KontrolÃ¼ BaÅŸlÄ±yor..."

VIOLATIONS=0

# Lint kontrolÃ¼
echo ""
echo "ğŸ¨ Lint kontrolÃ¼..."
./gradlew lintDebug > /dev/null 2>&1
LINT_RESULT=$?

if [ $LINT_RESULT -eq 0 ]; then
    echo "   âœ… Lint kontrolÃ¼ baÅŸarÄ±lÄ±"
else
    echo "   âŒ Lint hatalarÄ± tespit edildi"
    ((VIOLATIONS++))
fi

# Gizli bilgi sÄ±zÄ±ntÄ±sÄ± kontrolÃ¼
echo ""
echo "ğŸ•µï¸ Gizli bilgi sÄ±zÄ±ntÄ±sÄ± kontrolÃ¼..."

# API key, token, password gibi hassas bilgiler
SENSITIVE_PATTERNS=(
    "API_KEY.*=.*['\"]([A-Za-z0-9]{20,})['\"]"
    "PASSWORD.*=.*['\"](.+)['\"]"
    "SECRET.*=.*['\"](.+)['\"]"
    "TOKEN.*=.*['\"](.+)['\"]"
    "aws_access_key_id"
    "private_key"
)

SECRET_FOUND=0
for pattern in "${SENSITIVE_PATTERNS[@]}"; do
    RESULTS=$(git grep -iE "$pattern" -- '*.kt' '*.java' '*.xml' '*.json' 2>/dev/null)
    if [ -n "$RESULTS" ]; then
        echo "   âš ï¸  Potansiyel gizli bilgi tespit edildi:"
        echo "$RESULTS"
        ((SECRET_FOUND++))
    fi
done

if [ $SECRET_FOUND -eq 0 ]; then
    echo "   âœ… Gizli bilgi sÄ±zÄ±ntÄ±sÄ± tespit edilmedi"
else
    echo "   âŒ $SECRET_FOUND potansiyel gizli bilgi tespit edildi"
    ((VIOLATIONS++))
fi

# TODO ve FIXME kontrolÃ¼
echo ""
echo "ğŸ“ TODO/FIXME kontrolÃ¼..."
TODO_COUNT=$(git grep -iE "TODO|FIXME" -- '*.kt' '*.java' | wc -l)

if [ $TODO_COUNT -gt 0 ]; then
    echo "   âš ï¸  $TODO_COUNT adet TODO/FIXME bulundu"
    echo "   (Bu hata deÄŸil, bilgi amaÃ§lÄ±dÄ±r)"
else
    echo "   âœ… TODO/FIXME bulunamadÄ±"
fi

# SONUÃ‡
echo ""
echo "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•"
if [ $VIOLATIONS -eq 0 ]; then
    echo "âœ… BAÅARILI: Kod kalitesi ve gÃ¼venlik kontrolÃ¼ geÃ§ildi"
    echo "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•"
    exit 0
else
    echo "âŒ BAÅARISIZ: $VIOLATIONS adet kalite/gÃ¼venlik ihlali tespit edildi"
    echo "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•"
    exit 1
fi
```

## ğŸ”— CI/CD ENTEGRASYONU

### GitHub Actions Workflow

```yaml
name: PATIDOST Titan Core Validation

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main, develop ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main, develop ]

jobs:
  validate:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    
    steps:
    - name: Checkout kodu
      uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
    - name: Script'lere Ã§alÄ±ÅŸtÄ±rma izni ver
      run: chmod +x scripts/*.sh
      
    - name: Titan Core Validation
      run: ./scripts/validate_titan_core.sh
      
    - name: Validation Raporu YÃ¼kle
      if: always()
      uses: actions/upload-artifact@v3
      with:
        name: validation-reports
        path: evidence/VALIDATION_*.txt
```
